overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑎</text></svg></div></span></span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); We want to see if we can make a total&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑛</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.497em" height="0.449em" viewBox="0 -0.441 0.497 0.449" style="vertical-align: -0.008em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑛</text></svg></div></span></span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑟</text></svg></div></span></span>, you&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">must</span>&nbsp;start with the specific multiple of&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; Let’s call that starting multiple&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msub><mi>𝐵</mi><mi>𝑟</mi></msub></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.043em" height="0.903em" viewBox="0 -0.653 1.043 0.903" style="vertical-align: -0.25em; font-size: 0.75px" transform="translate(0.696,0.25)">𝑟</text></svg></div></span></span>, you can make&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">every single number larger than it</span>&nbsp;in that same remainder group simply by adding&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑎</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.502em" height="0.451em" viewBox="0 -0.441 0.502 0.451" style="vertical-align: -0.01em; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.2222,0)">+</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.1294,0)">5</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="2.2406em" height="0.684em" viewBox="0 -0.676 2.2406 0.684" style="vertical-align: -0.008em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.2778,0)">=</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.2406,0)">2</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.7406,0)">7</text></svg></div></span></span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The "Unlock":</span>&nbsp;Once you have enough&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑏</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.47em" height="0.679em" viewBox="0 -0.668 0.47 0.679" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑏</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;coins to reach&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit; color: rgb(255, 137, 126);">any</em>&nbsp;number with a specific remainder, you have "unlocked" that remainder forever. You can reach&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">every larger number</span>&nbsp;with that same remainder simply by stacking more and more&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑎</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.502em" height="0.451em" viewBox="0 -0.441 0.502 0.451" style="vertical-align: -0.01em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑎</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;coins on top of it.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ol><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Why this proves the "Largest Gap":<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The "starting point" for each remainder group is the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">smallest</span>&nbsp;multiple of&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑏</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.47em" height="0.679em" viewBox="0 -0.668 0.47 0.679" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>12</mn></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1em" height="0.676em" viewBox="0 -0.676 1 0.676" style="vertical-align: 0em; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.5,0)">2</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;is the smallest number with remainder&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1em" height="0.676em" viewBox="0 -0.676 1 0.676" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">7 has the right remainder, but we don't have enough "value" to reach it using our coins.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); Therefore, every single number after that point already has an "unlocked" ladder it can climb.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: Why&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); If you take the first&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑎</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.502em" height="0.451em" viewBox="0 -0.441 0.502 0.451" style="vertical-align: -0.01em; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow><mn>0</mn><mi>𝑏</mi></mrow></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.97em" height="0.69em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.97 0.69" style="vertical-align: -0.014em; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.5,0)">𝑏</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;up to&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Once you've used&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>𝑎</mi></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.502em" height="0.451em" viewBox="0 -0.441 0.502 0.451" style="vertical-align: -0.01em; Any further multiple (like&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow><mi>𝑎</mi><mi>𝑏</mi></mrow></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.972em" height="0.679em" viewBox="0 -0.668 0.972 0.679" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑎</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.502,0)">𝑏</text></svg></div></span></span>) would just repeat a remainder you already have (<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow><mi>𝑎</mi><mi>𝑏</mi></mrow></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.972em" height="0.679em" viewBox="0 -0.668 0.972 0.679" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑎</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.502,0)">𝑏</text></svg></div></span></span>&nbsp;has remainder&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>0</mn></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.5em" height="0.69em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.5 0.69" style="vertical-align: -0.014em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">0</text></svg></div></span></span>, just like&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow><mn>0</mn><mi>𝑏</mi></mrow></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.97em" height="0.69em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.97 0.69" style="vertical-align: -0.014em; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.5,0)">𝑏</text></svg></div></span></span>).<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Why is&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><span style="display: inline;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">(</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.502em" height="0.451em" viewBox="0 -0.441 0.502 0.451" style="vertical-align: -0.01em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑎</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1.6294em" height="0.676em" viewBox="0 -0.676 1.6294 0.676" style="vertical-align: 0em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0.2222,0)">−</text><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(1.1294,0)">1</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.333em" height="0.853em" viewBox="0 -0.676 0.333 0.853" style="vertical-align: -0.177em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">)</text></svg></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="0.47em" height="0.679em" viewBox="0 -0.668 0.47 0.679" style="vertical-align: -0.011em; overflow: visible; user-select: none;"><text fill="#E6E8F0" style="font-family: XITSMath-Regular; font-size: 1px" transform="translate(0,0)">𝑏</text></svg></div></span></span></span>&nbsp;the "latest"?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; white-space: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); Because&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden; position: absolute; user-select: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>12</mn></math></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" direction="ltr" width="1em" height="0.676em" viewBox="0 -0.676 1 0.676" style="vertical-align: 0em; Since there are&nbsp;<span style="display: inline;"><span style="font-size: 1.15em;"><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"><div style="inset: 0px; opacity: 0.001; overflow: hidden;
